info:Stayed in June 2024
info:Family
info:2 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted June 10, 2024
msg:We came with our 20-month old toddler for a staycation during the long weekend. We upgraded to the club room and the service and amenities were worth it. Even though it rained on both days, there were plenty to do at the hotel. All three of us had a nice soak in the large bathtub in our room when it rained hard outside. The room was spacious and clean, and the bed was huge and comfortable. The hotel was very thoughtful to have even left a child-size slippers, children dental kits, and a toddler mattress in the room. When it wasn't raining, our boy really enjoyed himself at the beach, indoor pool (and hot tub), and the waterpark, and so did we. There was also a huge outdoor playground by Joy Kids that featured several activity hubs like climbs and slides, foam construction blocks, and a merry-go-round ride. The breakfast at Mercado had a great spread that included cold cuts and cheeses, great coffees, freshly squeeze juices, and delightful pastries. We had nice simple afternoon teas and a more lavish evening cocktails at the club, but you should arrive earlier in the evenings to enjoy the full spread. Ms Jennifer was attentive and helpful when we were there and also helped us with a pleasant check-out. We highly recommend this place for families with young children.

The bathtub is  large, which comes with a view .  The room has a balcony with a view of the swimming pool  and a glimpse of  " China Splendid".   When you arrive your room, you will exclaim with "wows" and  feel relaxing when you step out to the balcony.

We paid the room rate together with breakfast, whch is cheaper than you buy separately,    It's conveneient to eat there and head out to  the swimming pools and sight-seeing.  The buffet  has  a wide seletcion of  food.  It has freshly squeezed juice - it's  very rare to see now.   I must give a thumb up to the two staffs, who are busy squeeziing juices to all those demaning customers.

The swimming pool with slides and waterfun activies are in the shade.  Even though  it's even blazing hot outside,  you can still enjoy and have fun.  It's prefect for us.  My children do not want too thrilling slides.    I also don't want my heart to beat too fast!   Another huge pool is very relaxing to swim , float and there's  a pool bar.

We went to Go-Kart on our last day,  whcih was $10 Taxi drive.  My teenage son had a blast.  Thank you very much to the Cconcierge Kevin, who helped us to check whether it was open and get a cheaper rate on the App.  

I would strongly recommend to this hotel for a relaxing weekend  with the kids.   You can defintly chill out.     When you stay in Shenzhen hotels,  you can always expect 5-star services.   InterContinental  Shenzhen certainly lives up to the expection with a fraction of the price.

name:C‚Äçh‚Äçe‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äçf‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äçy‚Äçu‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äç‚Ñ¢

posted:Posted June 7, 2024
msg:Shenzhen OCT InterContinental Hotel Pool View One-Bedroom Suite: Wandering in the Caribbean
üõè „ÄêÔ∏è Shenzhen OCT InterContinental Hotel Accommodation Guide„Äë

üìå Hotel Overview Overview

‚ù∂. Comprehensive evaluation: There are 59 InterContinental brand hotels in China (including Taiwan Province and Hong Kong Special Administrative Region). The suffix of their names is generally "InterContinental Hotel" or "InterContinental Resort Hotel", but there are exceptions, such as: InterContinental Hotel Jiuzhai Paradise, InterContinental Hotel Chengdu Global Center Paradise, InterContinental Hotel Lhasa Holy Land Paradise, InterContinental Hotel Chengdu Century City Paradise, Jinjiang Tomson Hotel, InterContinental Hotel Shenzhen OCT... The reason why these hotels have special names is that the first four are because they all belong to the same Chinese owner (Sunac Cultural Tourism, which is the original Yunnan Tourism Investment and the earliest Century City Convention and Exhibition), which is a unified, local "separatist" name; the reason for the latter two is that the guest rooms are large in size and they are benchmark legendary hotels in the region in terms of historical status and building complex itself. Therefore, living around InterContinental OCT, you will feel that this is a self-contained independent community with a strong tourism and business atmosphere. For 18 years, this has been the source of youth for Shennan Avenue; 
‚ù∑. Brief description of the location: There are 97 central enterprises in China, and three of them are headquartered in Shenzhen, including China Electronics at the vice-ministerial level, and OCT and CGN at the bureau level. The Happy Valley and Window of the World tourist area where OCT InterContinental is located is one of the ultimate destinations for any tourist who goes to Guangdong to check in.

üè® About the guest room In Room

‚ù∂. Guest room layout: The hotel arranged a 75-square-meter executive single-bedroom king-size bed suite with pool view for me, which is second only to the 688-square-meter presidential suite, hidden room type, 130-square-meter garden duplex suite, and 106-square-meter Chinese suite. In addition to a wide variety of foreign channels (the hotel has a very high proportion of foreign guests), there is also a "Movie World" to choose from, and the film library is huge. The balcony is very comfortable and the scenery is invincible (the surrounding greenery is too good, don't forget, the city with the most parks in China is Shenzhen, so envious), and the bathtub is big enough for two children to play;
‚ù∑. Welcome gift: The fruit plate is exquisite and rich enough, as if you are on the tropical island of St. Kitts and Nevis. San Aino sparkling mineral water is also from Spain, full of details!

‚òïÔ∏è Dining

‚ù∂. Gourmet glimpse: The milkshake in the all-day restaurant is the highlight, a magic weapon to seduce taste buds; pineapple buns are of course the most authentic in Guangdong;
‚ù∑. City gluttony: Turn right and you will reach Exit C of the "Overseas Chinese Town" subway station, which is convenient for eating anywhere (in fact, there are a lot of business groups around the hotel, which can fully meet your various taste needs);
‚ù∏. Executive Lounge: The breakfast a la carte menu is rich in variety, and the white-cut chicken and soft European bread during happy hour are my favorites. There are outdoor areas and ambassador/royal ambassador private areas. This flaming red lip-style color scheme spreads from the suite to every corner of the lounge and lobby public area. It is passionate, unrestrained, and free and easy, and it always highlights the Spanish and Caribbean themes. The lounge (business center) and the suite I stayed in are at the two ends of the same floor, ensuring the quietness and privacy of the guest room.

üèä Hardware Facilities

‚ù∂. Hotel environment: Because it is deep in the tourist destination building complex, the hotels built by OCT here are completely integrated into the context and vacation culture. The Venice Indigo focuses on the Italian water city culture, and the OCT InterContinental focuses on the Caribbean style and rich Spanish culture. This upstream and downstream differentiated layout is similar to the Universal Studios Grand Hotel and NUO Hotel in Beijing Universal Studios, and the Toy Story Hotel and Paradise Hotel in Shanghai Disney Resort. No matter which ethnic group you come from, you can find a place to live that suits you, and they are all close to the scenic area. Take the InterContinental OCT for example. From the guest rooms to the public areas, from the sculptures and decorative paintings to the coffee cup patterns and room colors, all highlight the bullfighting culture, as if you are in the streets of Madrid or the Caribbean countries, full of exotic customs, saving you from going abroad - this was a very popular practice at the time, such as Beijing's World Park and Shenzhen's Window of the World. After all, at the beginning of reform and opening up, on the one hand, people were eager to communicate, integrate and integrate with foreign cultures; on the other hand, most people still did not have the financial resources to go abroad, and this type of resort filled this gap; 
‚ù∑. Recreation and fitness: After the college entrance examination, summer vacation is coming. Soon, the national hotel industry will usher in the traditional "swimming pool season (money-making season)", and the leader in this regard is naturally InterContinental OCT. The swimming pool is divided into two areas, indoor and outdoor. It is open until 12 o'clock in the evening, fully meeting the needs of family happiness. The pirate ship "intrudes" in the scene, which further highlights the gracefulness and fantasy of the fairy tale world. No child will dislike it;
‚ù∏. Children's play: Utopia Amusement Club is one of its characteristics. It is similar to a miniature version of Club Med hosting. Babies like it very much.

üåü Unforgettable Moments the Moments
‚ù∂. Star employee: Manager Kan (Hina) has been taking care of me meticulously throughout my stay. From the communication before check-in to the comprehensive arrangements during check-in, I deeply felt that IC's "continental" and warm encounter are so beautiful. Thank you! Guo Zihao (Alan) from the front office department is a handsome guy from Xi'an, the ancient capital of 13 dynasties. His peerless appearance is hard to find in any seven-star platinum diamond hotel next to InterContinental, not to mention. He has the potential to join an idol group. Besides being handsome, his professional ability is also comparable. He arranged everything for me perfectly, saving me a lot of unnecessary energy and time. Thank you! The bellboys' attire is a major feature: OCT InterContinental mainly has male bellboys in bullfighter costumes; Venice Indigo has both male and female bellboys in sailor suits, which gives a strong sense of immersion;
‚ù∑. Number of stays: I have stayed in this hotel 9 times, and this is the 10th time;
‚ù∏. Tips: I often host performances at the nearby Spring Cocoon Sports Center (such as the Nanshan Pop Music Festival musical special, etc.) or watch performances in the IHG box upstairs as an audience (such as Mo Xi Zi Shi/Hu Defu/Haomeimei folk music concerts, etc.). Based on the principle of proximity, InterContinental Group will choose the ticket collection location at OCT InterContinental Concierge. After you get the ticket, you can drive to the performance. It is very close; also because it is close to the performance venue, the grassroots staff participating in the performance generally stay at Donghua Holiday Inn, while the participating stars/artists/guests choose to stay at OCT InterContinental, so the star-studded rate of this IC is very high. The food and drinks in the private rooms are generally provided by Donghua Holiday Catering Department; the same is true in Beijing, where the food in the private rooms of Huaxi Live InterContinental is generally provided by the nearby Southwest Huayu.

üìç Brief summary Conclusion

‚ù∂. Wonderful moments: Due to its superior geographical location, good reputation, and safe and reliable background of central enterprises, OCT InterContinental is often the designated foreign guest reception hotel by the municipal government and the district government (Nanshan). During my stay, I encountered a number of foreign affairs activities visited by VIPs from the Middle East. As expected, there is a reason why these VIPs always choose to stay at OCT InterContinental. From the security team to the front desk reception, every member of the hotel looks like they have received meticulous, long-term, and efficient training. Their words and deeds are so "silky" and decent, and they are comfortable to look at;
‚ù∑. Regrets: It would be more perfect if the cocktails in the lounge had more varieties. Of course, it is already very good now. There is a "Bullfighting" made with coffee-based liquor, which once again highlights the theme of the hotel and is worthy of appreciation;
‚ù∏. Questions and Answers: A friend asked why Shanghai Greenland Marriott changed to an office building? A: Nowadays, all walks of life are in a fierce competition, including the automobile industry, the real estate industry, the hotel industry and the tourism industry. Today, the hotel market in mainland China has long entered the era of destocking, and there will be more and more cases of survival of the fittest. Hotels like OCT InterContinental, which have both internal and external cultivation, hard work in service, and the support of big trees, will naturally stand firm for a long time.
